***libertijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:libertijn.html>libertijn</a> (91240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">libertin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">libertīnus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijn.html>libertijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijnen.html>libertijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:libertijn.html>libertijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">libertine</span>, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> loose morals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A religious dissenter who didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> adhere to Protestant (usually Reformed) orthodoxy; often used of Anabaptists, more loosely also of Remonstrants.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">licence</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licentia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">license</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licens</i>, present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">licere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be allowed, be allowable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***lichaam.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichaam.html>lichaam</a> (590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lichame</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lechame</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lichamo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līkahamô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">body, bodily frame, corpse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">body, lich</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">haam</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">covering, cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***licht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> (765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*linhtaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁lengʷʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichter.html>lichter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lichtst.html>lichtst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>light, of little weight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> easy, mild</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laaien.html>laai</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lichterloh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ablaze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl">in <a href = vnd.unilang:lichterlaaie.html>lichterlaaie</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:lichterlaaie.html>lichterlaaie</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:lichterlaaie.html>lichterlaaie</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ablaze
<dl><dd><i>Hendrix <a href = vnd.unilang:zette.html>zette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fender.html>Fender</a> Stratocaster <b>in <a href = vnd.unilang:lichterlaaie.html>lichterlaaie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdens.html>tijdens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:optreden.html>optreden</a> in 1967 in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Londense Astoria.</i><sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.parool.nl/parool/nl/23/muziek/article/detail/30706/2008/09/04/Gitaar-Hendrix-brengt-ruim-drie-ton-op.dhtml">[1]</a></sup>  |  Hendrix set the <a href = vnd.unilang:fender.html>Fender</a> Stratocaster <i>ablaze</i> during a performance in 1967 in the Astoria in London.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***lichtsabel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichtsabel.html>lichtsabel</a> (103724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A loan translation of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lightsaber</i>. A compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">light</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sabel.html>sabel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">saber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-zinnig</i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">leichtsinnig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frivolous, unserious</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lidmaat.html>lidmaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lidmaat.html>lidmaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lidmaat.html>lidmaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a> (2679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liet.html>liet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lioth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leuþą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lied.html>lied</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liederen.html>liederen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liedje.html>liedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>song</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:liederen.html>liederen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now chiefly restricted to solemn <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a>, such as hymns or anthems. Otherwise the plural diminutive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liedjes.html>liedjes</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used. (The singular <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also more often than not replaced with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:liedje.html>liedje</a></i> when referring to a “mundane” song.)
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijdlied.html>strijdlied</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">treurlied</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volkslied.html>volkslied</a></span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:muzikale.html>muzikale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekst.html>tekst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> verklankt, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> vormgegeven in <a href = vnd.unilang:couplet.html>couplet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:refrein.html>refrein</a>

***lieden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a> (15795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liede</i>, originally a singular collective noun. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*liudi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liudiz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lout</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lede.html>lede</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">leod</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leute</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)

***liefhebben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebben.html>liefhebben</a> (6039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebben.html>liefhebben</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lief.html>lief</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">leefhebben</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">liebhaben</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebben.html>liefhebben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to love (to have a strong affection for)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a></i>. <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lover, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:loves.html>loves</a> someone or something</li></ol>

***lieveheersbeestje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lieveheersbeestje.html>lieveheersbeestje</a> (40564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lieve.html>Lieve</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>Heer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">our Dear Lord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beestje.html>beestje</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beast, animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg/250px-Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="190" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg/375px-Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg/500px-Calvia_quatuordecimguttata01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="902" data-file-height="686" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Roomvleklieveheersbeestje</i><br />Cream-dotted ladybug</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieveheersbeestje.html>lieveheersbeestje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieveheersbeestjes.html>lieveheersbeestjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ladybird.html>ladybird</a>, ladybug, insectivore beetle of the family Coccinellidae</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">onzelieveheersbeestje</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">pimpampoen</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Belgium</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lieveheersbeestje.html>lieveheersbeestje</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <i><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">dim. tant.</span></i>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ligjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*legʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie; to be lying down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often of place names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be, to be placed or located
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rommel.html>rommel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zolder.html>zolder</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> a lot of rubbish in the attic.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> Geldrop <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Could you tell <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> where Geldrop <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> (located)</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> an implication of lying, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biefstuk.html>biefstuk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Your <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> (lying)</b> there getting cold.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ligging.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a> (30421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ligginge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>liggingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>geographical position, stressing in particular the relation to the surroundings or the orientation of an object; location, lie, situation</li>
<li>the position of an unborn mammal in the womb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the act or state of lying, reclination</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">achterhoofdligging</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">buikligging</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">dwarsligging</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kruinligging</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liggingsafwijking</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">rugligging</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuitligging.html>stuitligging</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">zijligging</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
